Some\nof the famous IT companies in Pune are Tata Consultancy Services, Infosys, Tech Mahindra, KPIT\nCummins, Wipro etc. Apart from this, there are around 400 colleges in Pune and some of the\ntop engineering colleges are Pune Institute of Computer Technology, Bharti Vidyapeeth\nUniversity College of Engineering, Symbiosis Institute of Technology and many more.\nLiving in Pune is very affordable as the property rates in Pune are reasonable. Even the famous\nbuilders in Pune are offering residential projects in Pune at affordable prices. of\nMaharashtra. Being the second greenest capital in India, Pune maintains its cleanliness and\nbeauty with lush green trees on the roadside and non- bumpy roads. Pune climate remains\nmoderate as it never gets too cold or too hot and never disappoints your mood and the city is\nusually cold and windy.\nPune is attracting many IT companies to establish their....Read more\nPune is the seventh most famous city in India and the second largest city in the Indian state of\nMaharashtra. Being the second greenest capital in India, Pune maintains its cleanliness and\nbeauty with lush green trees on the roadside and non- bumpy roads. Pune climate remains\nmoderate as it never gets too cold or too hot and never disappoints your mood and the city is\nusually cold and windy.\nPune is attracting many IT companies to establish their corporate and base offices here.
